PER_SYR = {
	per_intervene_SYR = {
		allowed = { tag = PER }

		available = {
			or = {
				SYR = { has_volunteers_amount_from = { tag = PER count > 0 } }
				FSA = { has_volunteers_amount_from = { tag = PER count > 0 } }
				NUS = { has_volunteers_amount_from = { tag = PER count > 0 } }
				ISI = { has_volunteers_amount_from = { tag = PER count > 0 } }
			}

		}

		activation = {
			SYR = {
				or = {
					has_war_with = ISI
					has_war_with = FSA
					has_war_with = NUS
					has_war_with = ROJ
				}
			}
		}

		is_good = yes

		selectable_mission = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 60
		days_remove = 5

		fire_only_once = yes


		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout per_intervene_SYR"
			add_political_power = -25
		}


		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision per_intervene_SYR"
			add_political_power = 25
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

PER_soleimani = {
	PER_mount_international_pressure = {

		icon = decision_generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			original_tag = PER
		}

		cost = 20
		days_remove = 3
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_mount_international_pressure"
			add_political_power = 40
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = mount_international_pressure
			USA = {
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
	PER_complain_to_the_united_nations = {

		icon = decision_generic_decision

		visible = {
			original_tag = PER
			has_country_flag = mount_international_pressure
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 15
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_complain_to_the_united_nationss"
			add_war_support = 0.02
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = complain_to_the_united_nations
			USA = {
				add_political_power = -75
			}
		}
	}
	PER_propaganda_in_shia_countries = {

		icon = boost_dec

		visible = {
			original_tag = PER
			has_country_flag = complain_to_the_united_nations
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { treasury > 1.4 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = cost_1_5

		days_remove = 5
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_propaganda_in_shia_countries"
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = propaganda_in_shia_countries
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = shia
					NOT = { original_tag = PER }
					has_opinion = { target = PER value > -50 }
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = USA
					modifier = assasinated_qasem_soleimani
				}
				add_ideas = qasem_soleimani_spirit
			}
		}
	}
	PER_fund_iraqi_allies = {

		icon = GFX_decision_recruit_operative

		visible = {
			original_tag = PER
		}

		cost = 50
		days_remove = 15
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_fund_iraqi_allies"

			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {

		}
	}

		}

						}
					}
				}
				50 = {

				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}

		}

	PER_iraq_mission_open = {
		allowed = {
			tag = PER
		}

		available = {
			original_tag = PER
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mission_country_selected }
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = mission_country_selected }
			OR = {
				KUR = {
					israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes
				}
				IRQ = {
					israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}

		icon = GFX_decision_iraq

		days_re_enable = 0
		fire_only_once = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_iraq_mission_open"
			set_variable = { PER_mission_country = IRQ }
			set_country_flag = mission_country_selected
			set_country_flag = mission_country_iraq
		}
	}

			tag = PER
		}

	PER_launch_missile = {
		allowed = {
			tag = PER
		}

		available = {
			original_tag = PER
			has_country_flag = mission_country_selected
			NOT = {
				has_decision = PER_launch_drone_attack
				has_decision = PER_capture_israeli_officials
				has_decision = PER_assassinate_israeli_agents
				has_decision = PER_ask_hashd_al_shaabi_to_raid_israeli_bases
				has_decision = PER_ask_houthis_to_raid_israeli_bases
				has_decision = PER_ask_huseyniyyun_to_raid_israeli_bases
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				var:PER_mission_country = {
					israel_has_more_than_1_influence_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = mission_country_selected
		}

		icon = GFX_decision_launch_missile

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^11 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^12 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^13 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^14 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^15 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^16 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^17 > 4}
				check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^18 > 4}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = PER_launch_missile_tt

		days_remove = 10
		days_re_enable = 100
		fire_only_once = no

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_5_icbm_tt
			if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^11 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^11 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^12 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^12 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^13 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^13 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^14 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^14 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^15 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^15 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^16 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^16 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^17 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^17 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = {missile_inventory_array^18 > 4} } subtract_from_variable = { var = missile_inventory_array^18 value = 5 } } #Removes 5 ICBM missiles
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision PER_launch_missile"
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ISR }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = PER_mission_country }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = {
					var = PER_mission_country
					value = IRQ
					compare = equals
				} }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ISR }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = KUR }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = {
					var = PER_mission_country
					value = AFG
					compare = equals
				} }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ISR }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TAL }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = {
					var = PER_mission_country
					value = ARM
					compare = equals
				} }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ISR }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = NKR }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = {
					var = PER_mission_country
					value = LEB
					compare = equals
				} }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ISR }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = HEZ }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = {
					var = PER_mission_country
					value = YEM
					compare = equals
				} }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -1 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ISR }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = HOU }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}

			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 1.0
				name = missile_attack_threat
			}
		}
	}
	PER_launch_drone_attack = {

PER_self_humiliation = {
	PER_seda_o_sima_propaganda = {

		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 120
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = { treasury > 1.4 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = cost_1_5
		icon = boost_dec

		visible = {
			AND = {
				has_completed_focus = PER_start_the_islamic_propaganda
				OR = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
				}
			}
		}
		allowed = {
			original_tag = PER
		}
		available = {
			#check_variable = { treasury < 2 }
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_road_billboard_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_social_media_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level
					has_country_flag = PER_tehran_military_parade_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_shiraz_military_parade_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_mashhad_military_parade_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_ahvaz_military_parade_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_tabriz_military_parade_decision
					has_country_flag = PER_isfahan_military_parade_decision
				}
			}
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					var = islamic_propaganda_status
					value = 100
					compare = less_than
				}
				OR = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -1.5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = PER_seda_o_sima_decision
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = islamic_propaganda_status
				value = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = islamic_propaganda_status
						value = 100
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = { islamic_propaganda_status = 100 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = PER_seda_o_sima_decision
		}
	}

	PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level = {

		icon = fist_dec

		days_remove = 5
		days_re_enable = 3
		cost = 200

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = PER_start_the_islamic_propaganda
			OR = {
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
			}

		}
		allowed = {
			original_tag = PER
		}
		available = {
			#check_variable = { treasury < 5 }
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = PER_seda_o_sima_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_road_billboard_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_social_media_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_tehran_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_shiraz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_mashhad_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_ahvaz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_tabriz_military_parade_decision
						has_country_flag = PER_isfahan_military_parade_decision
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = islamic_propaganda_status
						value = 100
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level_decision
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = {
				var = islamic_propaganda_status
				value = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_10
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_9
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_8
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_7
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_6
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_5
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_4
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_3
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_2
					add_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = PER_self_humiliation_idea_1
					add_idea = PER_unity_of_the_nation
				}
			}
			clear_variable = islamic_propaganda_status
			set_variable = { islamic_propaganda_status = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = PER_decrease_self_humiliation_level_decision
		}
	}
}

	PER_prepare_shia_rebellionsQ_9 = { #Timer QATAR

		fire_only_once = yes
		priority = 10
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = PER_Q
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = PER_free_shia2
				has_country_flag = PER_no_free_shia2
			}
		}

		allowed = {
		}

		available = {
			QAT = {
				amount_manpower_in_deployment_queue < 1
				has_army_manpower = {
					size > 3999
				}
				army_manpower_in_state = {
					amount > 3999
					state = 181
				}
				181 = {
					resistance < 50
				}
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 100
		is_good = no
		complete_effect = {
			QAT = {
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = -0.05
				clr_country_flag = PER_no_free_shia2
				set_country_flag = PER_qatar_fail
				add_state_core = 181
			}
			PER = {
				clr_country_flag = PER_free_shia2
				set_country_flag = PER_qatar_fail
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			QAT = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_war_support = -0.1
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = sunni
					add_idea = shia
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = wahabi_ulema
					add_idea = The_Ulema
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = saudi_royal_family
					add_idea = landowners
				}
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 4.0 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = QAT }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
				add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 8 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.4 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				clr_country_flag = PER_no_free_shia2
				set_country_flag = PER_qatar_success
				add_state_core = 181
			}
			PER = {
				clr_country_flag = PER_free_shia2
				set_country_flag = PER_qatar_success
			}
		}
	}

#The secret secret
form_HRM_category = {
	### Integrate ###
	#HRM
	HRM_formable = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		cost = 150
		days_remove = 365
		ai_will_do = { factor = 10 }
		allowed = {
		}
		available = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						HRM = {
						owns_state = 179
						owns_state = 978
						has_war = no
						}
					}
					AND = {
						PER = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							has_war = no
							owns_state = 978
						}
					}
					AND = {
						UAE = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							has_war = no
							owns_state = 179
						}
					}
				}
			}
		visible = {
			country_exists = HRM
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision HRM_formable"

			if = {
				limit = {
					HRM = { owns_state = 179 }
				}
				add_state_core = 179
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					UAE = { owns_state = 179 is_subject_of = ROOT}
				}
				add_state_core = 179
				annex_country = {
					target = UAE
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HRM = { owns_state = 978 }
				}
				add_state_core = 978
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PER = { owns_state = 978 is_subject_of = ROOT}
				}
				add_state_core = 978
				978 = {
					set_state_owner_to = HRM
					set_state_controller_to = HRM
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = {has_country_flag = is_HRM} }
				set_country_flag = is_HRM
			}
			set_country_flag = integrated_UAE
			set_cosmetic_tag = big_hrm
		}
	}

					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PER = {
							has_country_flag = five_time_equipment_HOU
						}
						YEM = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = negative_five_time_equipment_HOU
							}
						}
					}
					HOU	= {
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Inf_equipment
							amount = 1000
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = util_vehicle_0
							amount = 5000
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Anti_tank_0
							amount = 2500
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Anti_Air_1
							amount = 2500
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Strike_fighter2 #Su-24
							amount = 25
							producer = SOV
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PER = {
							has_country_flag = five_time_equipment_HOU
						}
						YEM = {
							has_country_flag = negative_five_time_equipment_HOU
						}
					}
					HOU	= {
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Inf_equipment
							amount = 7500
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = util_vehicle_0
							amount = 2500
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Anti_tank_0
							amount = 1450
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Anti_Air_1
							amount = 1450
							producer = PER
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = Strike_fighter2 #Su-24
							amount = 25
							producer = SOV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
PER_trade_spies = { #need
	trade_american_spy = {
		visible = {
			original_tag = PER

			has_completed_focus = PER_trade_spies_with_money
		}

		available = {
			has_captured_operative = USA
		}
		icon = usa

		cost = 0
		days_remove = 20
		fire_only_once = no

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision trade_american_spy"
		}

		remove_effect = {
			USA = { country_event = PER_spies_trade.1 }
		}
	}
